<aside

<p
class="title">about</p>









<p
class="bio">
After
surfacing
in
2000
with
the
breakthrough
single
&quot;Yellow,&quot;
Coldplay
quickly
became
one
of
the
biggest
bands
of
the
new
millennium,
honing
a
mix
of
introspective
Brit-pop
and
anthemic
rock
that
landed
the
British
quartet
a
near-permanent
residence...
</p>









<a
href="/coldplay/bio">read
more</a>








</aside>
